# Beta Conversations Operations [#beta/conversations]

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/conversations [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list]

_List all created conversations._

Retrieve a list of conversation entities sorted by creation time.

<ExpandableEntry slot="entry" id="type" parentId="ResponseFormat">

<div slot="title">

<Property typeInfo={{"label":"enum","linkedLabel":"enum","children":[{"label":"\"text\"","linkedLabel":"\"text\"","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"\"json_object\"","linkedLabel":"\"json_object\"","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"\"json_schema\"","linkedLabel":"\"json_schema\"","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}} typeAnnotations={[]}>

##### type [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+200+application-json+ModelConversation+completion_args+CompletionArgs+response_format+ResponseFormat+type]

</Property>

</div>

<div slot="content">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

</div>

</TabbedSection>

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/conversations [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start]

_Create a conversation and append entries to it._

Create a new conversation, using a base model or an agent and append entries. Completion and tool executions are run and the response is appended to the conversation.Use the returned conversation_id to continue the conversation.

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">

### Request Body [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+request]

<ExpandableEntry slot="entry" id="type" parentId="ResponseFormat">

<div slot="title">

<Property typeInfo={{"label":"enum","linkedLabel":"enum","children":[{"label":"\"text\"","linkedLabel":"\"text\"","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"\"json_object\"","linkedLabel":"\"json_object\"","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"\"json_schema\"","linkedLabel":"\"json_schema\"","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}} typeAnnotations={[]}>

##### type [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+request+completion_args+CompletionArgs+response_format+ResponseFormat+type]

</Property>

</div>

<div slot="content">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

</div>

</ExpandableEntry>

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/conversations/\{conversation\_id\} [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get]

_Retrieve a conversation information._

Given a conversation_id retrieve a conversation entity with its attributes.

<ExpandableEntry slot="entry" id="type" parentId="ResponseFormat">

<div slot="title">

<Property typeInfo={{"label":"enum","linkedLabel":"enum","children":[{"label":"\"text\"","linkedLabel":"\"text\"","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"\"json_object\"","linkedLabel":"\"json_object\"","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}},{"label":"\"json_schema\"","linkedLabel":"\"json_schema\"","children":[],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}],"breakoutSubTypes":{}}} typeAnnotations={[]}>

##### type [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+200+application-json+ModelConversation+completion_args+CompletionArgs+response_format+ResponseFormat+type]

</Property>

</div>

<div slot="content">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.

</div>

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/conversations/\{conversation\_id\} [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append]

_Append new entries to an existing conversation._

Run completion on the history of the conversation and the user entries. Return the new created entries.

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">

### Parameters [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append+parameters]

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content" variant="top-level">

##### conversation\_id <Pill variant="warning">required</Pill> [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append+parameters+conversation_id]

ID of the conversation to which we append entries.

</SectionContent>

</Section>

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">

</TabbedSection>

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/conversations/\{conversation\_id\}/history [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_history]

_Retrieve all entries in a conversation._

Given a conversation_id retrieve all the entries belonging to that conversation. The entries are sorted in the order they were appended, those can be messages, connectors or function_call.

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">

### Parameters [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_history+parameters]

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content" variant="top-level">

##### conversation\_id <Pill variant="warning">required</Pill> [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_history+parameters+conversation_id]

</SectionContent>

</Section>

</TabbedSection>

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>GET</b></Pill> /v1/conversations/\{conversation\_id\}/messages [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_messages]

_Retrieve all messages in a conversation._

Given a conversation_id retrieve all the messages belonging to that conversation. This is similar to retrieving all entries except we filter the messages only.

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">

### Parameters [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_history+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_messages+parameters]

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content" variant="top-level">

##### conversation\_id <Pill variant="warning">required</Pill> [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_history+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_messages+parameters+conversation_id]

</SectionContent>

</Section>

## <Pill variant="primary"><b>POST</b></Pill> /v1/conversations/\{conversation\_id\}/restart [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_restart]

_Restart a conversation starting from a given entry._

Given a conversation_id and an id, recreate a conversation from this point and run completion. A new conversation is returned with the new entries returned.

<Section variant="top-level">

<SectionTitle slot="title" variant="top-level">

### Parameters [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_history+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_messages+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_restart+parameters]

</SectionTitle>

<SectionContent slot="content" variant="top-level">

##### conversation\_id <Pill variant="warning">required</Pill> [#operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_list+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_start+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_get+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_append+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_history+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_messages+responses+operation-agents_api_v1_conversations_restart+parameters+conversation_id]

<div slot="content">

An object specifying the format that the model must output. Setting to `\{ "type": "json_object" \}` enables JSON mode, which guarantees the message the model generates is in JSON. When using JSON mode you MUST also instruct the model to produce JSON yourself with a system or a user message.
